$(window).scroll(function() {
    if ($(window).scrollTop() > 100) {
        // > 100px from top - show div

$('.header-wrap').addClass('small-header-wrap');
$('.body-container-wrapper').addClass('after-100')

    }
    else {
        // <= 100px from top - hide div
$('.header-wrap').removeClass( 'small-header-wrap' );
$('.body-container-wrapper').removeClass('after-100')
    }
});
</script>

<!-- Set Equal Height on Featured Nav -->
<script>
equalheight = function(container){

var currentTallest = 0,
     currentRowStart = 0,
     rowDivs = new Array(),
     $el,
     topPosition = 0;
 $(container).each(function() {

   $el = $(this);
   $($el).height('auto')
   topPostion = $el.position().top;

   if (currentRowStart != topPostion) {
     for (currentDiv = 0 ; currentDiv < rowDivs.length ; currentDiv++) {
       rowDivs[currentDiv].height(currentTallest);
     }
     rowDivs.length = 0; // empty the array
     currentRowStart = topPostion;
     currentTallest = $el.height();
     rowDivs.push($el);
   } else {
     rowDivs.push($el);
     currentTallest = (currentTallest < $el.height()) ? ($el.height()) : (currentTallest);
  }
   for (currentDiv = 0 ; currentDiv < rowDivs.length ; currentDiv++) {
     rowDivs[currentDiv].height(currentTallest);
   }
 });
}

$(window).load(function() {
  equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .bottom-nav-header h4');
equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col');

});


$(window).resize(function(){
  equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col');
equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .bottom-nav-header h4');


});

$( ".toggle-btn" ).click(function() {
  equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col');
equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .bottom-nav-header h4');
});

</script>
<!-- END Set Equal Height on Featured Nav -->

<!-- Convert Bootstrap Top Nav toggle to a dropdown -->
<script>
  var hoverTimeout;
  $('.dropdown-toggle').hover(
    function(){
      
      $(this).parent().addClass('open');
    },
    function(){
      $self=$(this);
      hoverTimeout=setTimeout(function(){
        $self.parent().removeClass('open');
      },190);
    }
  );
$(".dropdown-menu").hover(
  function(){
    clearTimeout(hoverTimeout);
  },
  function(){
    $(this).parent().removeClass('open');
  });
</script>
<!-- END Convert Bootstrap Top Nav toggle to a dropdown -->

<script>
$(window).load(function(){
	var boxes=$(".hs_blog_topics input, .hs_groups input");
	$(".hs_all_posts input").change(function(){
		if ($(this).is(":checked")){
			boxes.prop("checked",false);
		}
	});
	boxes.change(function(){
		if(boxes.filter(":checked").length==boxes.length){
			$(".hs_all_posts input").prop("checked",true);
			$(boxes).prop("checked",false);
		}
		else{
			$(".hs_all_posts input").prop("checked",false);
		}
	});

	$('.subscribe-form form').submit(function(event){
		
		if ($('.subscribe-form input[type="checkbox"]:checked').length==0){
                        event.preventDefault();
			$('.subscribe-form input[type="submit"]').before('<p class="error">Please select a newsletter to subscribe to.</p>');
		}
	});
});
</script>

    $('.svg-arrow-left').html(arrowLeft);

    var arrowUp = '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?><svg version="1.1" id="Layer_1" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" x="0px" y="0px" viewBox="0 0 22.4 11.6" enable-background="new 0 0 22.4 11.6" xml:space="preserve"><polygon points="11.2,0 0,11.6 22.4,11.6 "/></svg>';

    $('.svg-rating').each(function(){
       var starRating = $(this).data('star-rating');
       if(starRating){
        $(this).html(makeStars(starRating));
       }
    });

    $('.svg-rating.text-number').each(function(){
       var starRating = $(this).data('star-rating');
       if(starRating){
        $(this).html(makeStars(starRating))
            .append('<span class=\"number-rating\"><strong>' + starRating + '<\/strong><\/span>');
        
       }
    });
    
    $('.svg-rating.text-number.out-of-five').each(function(){
       var starRating = $(this).data('star-rating');
       if(starRating){
        $(this).html(makeStars(starRating))
            .append('<span class=\"number-rating\"><strong>' + starRating + '/5<\/strong><\/span>');
        
       }
    });


    function makeStars(rating){

        // rating should be out of 5
        var output = "";
      var ratings = [];
      var rating = rating || 0;
      var starNum =  [1,2,3,4,5];
    		for (var s in starNum){
              var num = 0;
              if(starNum[s] <= rating){
                num = 1;
              }
              if(starNum[s] > rating){
                num = 1 - (starNum[s] - rating);
                num = Math.round( num * 10) / 10;
                if (num<0){num=0}
              } 
              ratings.push(num*100);
    	}
    
    	for (var r in ratings){
    		var svg = '<span class="star"><svg version="1.1" id="star" x="0px" y="0px" viewBox="0 0 50 50" enable-background="new 0 0 50 50" xml:space="preserve"><polygon id="grey" fill="#ECEFF1" points="25 1.8 32.5 17.1 49.4 19.5 37.2 31.4 40.1 48.2 25 40.3 9.9 48.2 12.8 31.4 0.6 19.5 17.5 17.1 "/><g id="green"><defs><polygon id="XMLID_80_" points="25 1.8 32.5 17.1 49.4 19.5 37.2 31.4 40.1 48.2 25 40.3 9.9 48.2 12.8 31.4 0.6 19.5 17.5 17.1 "/></defs><clipPath id="starclip"><use xlink:href="#XMLID_80_"  overflow="visible"/></clipPath><rect id="rating-amount" clip-path="url(#starclip)" fill="#1DAB24" width="' + ratings[r] + '%" height="50"/></g></svg></span>';
    		output += svg;
    	}
      return output;
    }


});
</script>

$(document).ready(function(){

    var __wfm = __wfm || {};

    function createCookie(name,value,days) {
        if (days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
            var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
	    }
	    else var expires = "";
	    document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
	}

	function readCookie(name) {
	    var nameEQ = name + "=";
	    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	    for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
	        var c = ca[i];
	        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
	        if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
	    }
	    return null;
	}

	function eraseCookie(name) {
	    createCookie(name,"",-1);
	}



	
	
	$("body").on("activateQuickSignUp", function(){
		$('.quick-signup').each(function(){

			//activating forms
			var formInstanceId = Math.ceil(Math.random()*1000).toString();
			// var formName = 'quick-signup-form-target-module-' + formInstanceId;

<script>

$(document).ready(function(){

    function createCookie(name,value,days) {
	    if (days) {
	        var date = new Date();
	        date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
	        var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
	    }
	    else var expires = "";
	    document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
	}

	function readCookie(name) {
	    var nameEQ = name + "=";
	    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	    for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
	        var c = ca[i];
	        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
	        if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
	    }
	    return null;
	}

	function eraseCookie(name) {
	    createCookie(name,"",-1);
	}



// if click login button - create cookie


	$('.login-btn').click(function(){
		var isCustomer = readCookie("wfm_customer");
		if(!isCustomer){
			createCookie("wfm_customer","true",10);
		}
	});



});

</script>

    var nameEQ = name + "=";
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');

        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);

    }
    return null;
}

                clearInterval(interval);

    }

__wfm.event = function(obj, cb) {

    var str = JSON.stringify(obj);
    var email = __wfm.contact.email || '';

    var url = "https://wfm-marketing.herokuapp.com/events/log?event_name=";
    url += encodeURIComponent(str);
    url += "&email=";
    url += encodeURIComponent(email);
    url += "&utk=";
    url += encodeURIComponent(__wfm.readCookie('hubspotutk'));
    url += "&wfmid=";
    url += encodeURIComponent(__wfm.readCookie('__wfm_guid'));
    url += "&view_id=";
    url += encodeURIComponent(__wfm.pageViewId);
    
    // console.log(url);
    // console.log(obj);


    $.ajax({
        url: url,
        type: 'GET',
        complete: function(data, str) {
            if(cb){cb();}
        }
    });
}

__wfm.guid = function(){
    var existingCookie = __wfm.readCookie('__wfm_guid');
    // console.log('exco: '+existingCookie);
    if(!existingCookie){
    var d = new Date().getTime();
    if(window.performance && typeof window.performance.now === "function"){
        d += performance.now(); //use high-precision timer if available
    }
    var uuid = 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function(c) {
        var r = (d + Math.random()*16)%16 | 0;
        d = Math.floor(d/16);
        return (c=='x' ? r : (r&0x3|0x8)).toString(16);
    });
    (function(name,value,days) {
        if (days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
            var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
        }
        else var expires = "";
        document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
    })('__wfm_guid',uuid,3650);
    return uuid;
} else {
    return existingCookie;
}
    
}



__wfm.contact = {
    email: '',
    guid: __wfm.guid()
}



__wfm.starRating = function(rating){

    // rating should be out of 5
	var output = '<div class="star-rating-wrap">';
  var ratings = [];
  var rating = rating || 0;
  var starNum =  [1,2,3,4,5];
		for (var s in starNum){
          var num = 0;
          if(starNum[s] <= rating){
            num = 1;
          }
          if(starNum[s] > rating){
            num = 1 - (starNum[s] - rating);
            num = Math.round( num * 10) / 10;
            if (num<0){num=0}
          } 
          ratings.push(num*100);
	}

	for (var r in ratings){
		var svg = '<span class="star"><div class="star-solid-color" data-rating="' + ratings[r] +'" style="width:' + ratings[r] +'%;"></div><span class="wfm_icons-star wfm_icons ';
		if(ratings[r] >= 100){
			svg += 'wfm_icons-star-green"';	
		} else if (ratings[r] == 0){
			svg += 'wfm_icons-star-grey"';	
		} else {
			svg += 'wfm_icons-star-green" style="opacity:'+(ratings[r]/100)+';"';	
		}
		svg += '></span></span>';

		output += svg;
	}

	output += '</div>';
  return output;
}

$(document).ready(function(){
var __wfm = __wfm || {};
function createCookie(name,value,days) {
if (days) {
var date = new Date();
date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
}
else var expires = "";
document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
}
function readCookie(name) {
var nameEQ = name + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
var c = ca[i];
while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
}
return null;
}
function eraseCookie(name) {
createCookie(name,"",-1);
}

function makeStars(rating){
// rating should be out of 5
var output = "";
var ratings = [];
var rating = rating || 0;
var starNum =  [1,2,3,4,5];
for (var s in starNum){
var num = 0;
if(starNum[s] <= rating){
num = 1;
}
if(starNum[s] > rating){
num = 1 - (starNum[s] - rating);
num = Math.round( num * 10) / 10;
if (num<0){num=0}
} 
ratings.push(num*100);
}
for (var r in ratings){
var svg = '<span class="star"><svg version="1.1" id="star" x="0px" y="0px" viewBox="0 0 50 50" enable-background="new 0 0 50 50" xml:space="preserve"><polygon id="grey" fill="#ECEFF1" points="25 1.8 32.5 17.1 49.4 19.5 37.2 31.4 40.1 48.2 25 40.3 9.9 48.2 12.8 31.4 0.6 19.5 17.5 17.1 "/><g id="green"><defs><polygon id="XMLID_80_" points="25 1.8 32.5 17.1 49.4 19.5 37.2 31.4 40.1 48.2 25 40.3 9.9 48.2 12.8 31.4 0.6 19.5 17.5 17.1 "/></defs><clipPath id="starclip"><use xlink:href="#XMLID_80_"  overflow="visible"/></clipPath><rect id="rating-amount" clip-path="url(#starclip)" fill="#1DAB24" width="' + ratings[r] + '%" height="50"/></g></svg></span>';
output += svg;
}
return output;
}
});

<script>
equalheight = function(container){
var currentTallest = 0,
currentRowStart = 0,
rowDivs = new Array(),
$el,
topPosition = 0;
$(container).each(function() {
$el = $(this);
$($el).height('auto')
topPostion = $el.position().top;
if (currentRowStart != topPostion) {
for (currentDiv = 0 ; currentDiv < rowDivs.length ; currentDiv++) {
rowDivs[currentDiv].height(currentTallest);
}
rowDivs.length = 0; // empty the array
currentRowStart = topPostion;
currentTallest = $el.height();
rowDivs.push($el);
} else {
rowDivs.push($el);
currentTallest = (currentTallest < $el.height()) ? ($el.height()) : (currentTallest);
}
for (currentDiv = 0 ; currentDiv < rowDivs.length ; currentDiv++) {
rowDivs[currentDiv].height(currentTallest);
}
});
}
$(window).load(function() {
equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .bottom-nav-header h4');
equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col');
});
$(window).resize(function(){
equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col');
equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .bottom-nav-header h4');
});
$( ".toggle-btn" ).click(function() {
equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col');
equalheight('.features-bottom-nav .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .features-col .row-fluid-wrapper .row-fluid .bottom-nav-header h4');
});
</script>
<!-- END Set Equal Height on Featured Nav --></span>
</div><!--end layout-widget-wrapper -->
</div><!--end widget-span -->
</div><!--end row-->
</div><!--end row-wrapper -->
